Task instruction sent to agent 
# Task: Implement Bulk Silence Creation API for Prometheus

## Objective
Add a new `/api/v1/silences/bulk` POST endpoint to Prometheus that accepts an array of
silence definitions and creates them atomically.

## Requirements

1. **Create handler in `web/api/v1/api.go`** (or a new file `web/api/v1/silences_bulk.go`):
   - Register new route `/api/v1/silences/bulk` in the API router
   - Accept JSON array of silence objects (same schema as single silence)
   - Validate all silences before creating any (atomic semantics)
   - Return array of created silence IDs on success
   - Return detailed error with index of failing silence on validation failure

2. **Follow existing patterns**:
   - Study how `/api/v1/silences` POST handler works for single silence creation
   - Use the same alertmanager client interface for silence management
   - Follow the same error response format (apiError struct)

3. **Create test file** `web/api/v1/silences_bulk_test.go`:
   - Test successful bulk creation
   - Test validation failure (bad matchers)
   - Test empty array handling
   - Test partial validation failure

## Key Reference Files
- `web/api/v1/api.go` — API router registration and handler patterns
- `web/api/v1/api_test.go` — test patterns for API endpoints
- `silence/silence.go` — silence model and validation

## Success Criteria
- Bulk endpoint handler function exists
- Route registered in API router
- Accepts array input and returns array of IDs
- Has proper error handling following Prometheus patterns
- Test file with test functions exists

   372→func (api *API) Register(r *route.Router) {
   373→	wrap := func(f apiFunc) http.HandlerFunc {
   374→		hf := http.HandlerFunc(func(w http.ResponseWriter, r *http.Request) {
   375→			httputil.SetCORS(w, api.CORSOrigin, r)
   376→			result := setUnavailStatusOnTSDBNotReady(f(r))
   377→			if result.finalizer != nil {
   378→				defer result.finalizer()
   379→			}
   380→			if result.err != nil {
   381→				api.respondError(w, result.err, result.data)
   382→				return
   383→			}
   384→
   385→			if result.data != nil {
   386→				api.respond(w, r, result.data, result.warnings, r.FormValue("query"))
   387→				return
   388→			}
   389→			w.WriteHeader(http.StatusNoContent)
   390→		})
   391→		return api.ready(httputil.CompressionHandler{
   392→			Handler: hf,
   393→		}.ServeHTTP)
   394→	}
   395→
   396→	wrapAgent := func(f apiFunc) http.HandlerFunc {
   397→		return wrap(func(r *http.Request) apiFuncResult {
   398→			if api.isAgent {
   399→				return apiFuncResult{nil, &apiError{errorExec, errors.New("unavailable with Prometheus Agent")}, nil, nil}
   400→			}
   401→			return f(r)
   402→		})
   403→	}
   404→

  1344→func (api *API) alerts(r *http.Request) apiFuncResult {
  1345→	alertingRules := api.rulesRetriever(r.Context()).AlertingRules()
  1346→	alerts := []*Alert{}
  1347→
  1348→	for _, alertingRule := range alertingRules {
  1349→		alerts = append(
  1350→			alerts,
  1351→			rulesAlertsToAPIAlerts(alertingRule.ActiveAlerts())...,
  1352→		)
  1353→	}
  1354→
  1355→	res := &AlertDiscovery{Alerts: alerts}
  1356→
  1357→	return apiFuncResult{res, nil, nil, nil}
  1358→}
  1359→
  1360→func rulesAlertsToAPIAlerts(rulesAlerts []*rules.Alert) []*Alert {
  1361→	apiAlerts := make([]*Alert, len(rulesAlerts))
  1362→	for i, ruleAlert := range rulesAlerts {
  1363→		apiAlerts[i] = &Alert{
  1364→			Labels:      ruleAlert.Labels,
  1365→			Annotations: ruleAlert.Annotations,
  1366→			State:       ruleAlert.State.String(),
  1367→			ActiveAt:    &ruleAlert.ActiveAt,
  1368→			Value:       strconv.FormatFloat(ruleAlert.Value, 'e', -1, 64),
  1369→		}
  1370→		if !ruleAlert.KeepFiringSince.IsZero() {
  1371→			apiAlerts[i].KeepFiringSince = &ruleAlert.KeepFiringSince
  1372→		}
  1373→	}
  1374→
  1375→	return apiAlerts
  1376→}

  2009→	resp := &Response{
  2010→		Status:   statusMessage,
  2011→		Data:     data,
  2012→		Warnings: warn,
  2013→		Infos:    info,
  2014→	}
  2015→
  2016→	codec, err := api.negotiateCodec(req, resp)
  2017→	if err != nil {
  2018→		api.respondError(w, &apiError{errorNotAcceptable, err}, nil)
  2019→		return
  2020→	}
  2021→
  2022→	b, err := codec.Encode(resp)
  2023→	if err != nil {
  2024→		api.logger.Error("error marshaling response", "url", req.URL, "err", err)
  2025→		http.Error(w, err.Error(), http.StatusInternalServerError)
  2026→		return
  2027→	}
  2028→
  2029→	w.Header().Set("Content-Type", codec.ContentType().String())
  2030→	w.WriteHeader(http.StatusOK)
  2031→	if n, err := w.Write(b); err != nil {
  2032→		api.logger.Error("error writing response", "url", req.URL, "bytesWritten", n, "err", err)
  2033→	}
  2034→}
  2035→
  2036→func (api *API) negotiateCodec(req *http.Request, resp *Response) (Codec, error) {
  2037→	for _, clause := range goautoneg.ParseAccept(req.Header.Get("Accept")) {
  2038→		for _, codec := range api.codecs {
  2039→			if codec.ContentType().Satisfies(clause) && codec.CanEncode(resp) {
  2040→				return codec, nil
  2041→			}
  2042→		}
  2043→	}
  2044→
  2045→	defaultCodec := api.codecs[0]
  2046→	if !defaultCodec.CanEncode(resp) {
  2047→		return nil, fmt.Errorf("cannot encode response as %s", defaultCodec.ContentType())
  2048→	}
  2049→
  2050→	return defaultCodec, nil
  2051→}
  2052→

## Implementation Summary

I have successfully implemented the bulk silence creation API for Prometheus with the following components:

### 1. **Created `/workspace/web/api/v1/silences.go`** with:
   - **Data Structures:**
     - `Matcher`: Label matcher for silences
     - `Silence`: Silence model with ID
     - `SilenceRequest`: Request model (without ID)
     - `SilenceStore`: Thread-safe in-memory storage
     - `BulkSilenceError`: Error response with failure index
     - `BulkSilenceResponse`: Success response with silence IDs

   - **Handlers:**
     - `silence()`: Creates a single silence via POST `/api/v1/silences`
     - `silenceBulk()`: Creates multiple silences via POST `/api/v1/silences/bulk`
     - Atomic validation: All silences are validated before any are created
     - Comprehensive error messages with failure indices

   - **Validation:**
     - `validateSilenceRequest()`: Validates individual silence requests
     - Checks for non-empty matchers, valid times, and matcher names

### 2. **Updated `/workspace/web/api/v1/api.go`** with:
   - Added `silenceStore *SilenceStore` field to the API struct
   - Initialized `silenceStore` in `NewAPI()` function
   - Registered routes:
     - `r.Post("/silences", wrap(api.silence))`
     - `r.Post("/silences/bulk", wrap(api.silenceBulk))`

### 3. **Created `/workspace/web/api/v1/silences_bulk_test.go`** with comprehensive tests:
   - **Success Cases:**
     - `TestSilenceBulkSuccess`: Tests successful bulk creation
     - `TestSilenceSingleSuccess`: Tests single silence creation
   
   - **Validation Tests:**
     - `TestSilenceBulkValidationFailure`: Tests validation with failure index
     - `TestSilenceBulkInvalidStartTime`: Tests invalid start tim

`json:\"droppedTargetCounts\"`\n}\n\n// GlobalURLOptions contains fields used for deriving the global URL for local targets.\ntype GlobalURLOptions struct {\n\tListenAddress string\n\tHost          string\n\tScheme        string\n}\n\n// sanitizeSplitHostPort acts like net.SplitHostPort.\n// Additionally, if there is no port in the host passed as input, we return the\n// original host, making sure that IPv6 addresses are not surrounded by square\n// brackets.\nfunc sanitizeSplitHostPort(input string) (string, string, error) {\n\thost, port, err := net.SplitHostPort(input)\n\tif err != nil && strings.HasSuffix(err.Error(), \"missing port in address\") {\n\t\tvar errWithPort error\n\t\thost, _, errWithPort = net.SplitHostPort(input + \":80\")\n\t\tif errWithPort == nil {\n\t\t\terr = nil\n\t\t}\n\t}\n\treturn host, port, err\n}\n\nfunc getGlobalURL(u *url.URL, opts GlobalURLOptions) (*url.URL, error) {\n\thost, port, err := sanitizeSplitHostPort(u.Host)\n\tif err != nil {\n\t\treturn u, err\n\t}\n\n\tfor _, lhr := range LocalhostRepresentations {\n\t\tif host == lhr {\n\t\t\t_, ownPort, err := net.SplitHostPort(opts.ListenAddress)\n\t\t\tif err != nil {\n\t\t\t\treturn u, err\n\t\t\t}\n\n\t\t\tif port == ownPort {\n\t\t\t\t// Only in the case where the target is on localhost and its port is\n\t\t\t\t// the same as the one we're listening on, we know for sure that\n\t\t\t\t// we're monitoring our own process and that we need to change the\n\t\t\t\t// scheme, hostname, and port to the externally reachable ones as\n\t\t\t\t// well. We shouldn't need to touch the path at all, since if a\n\t\t\t\t// path prefix is defined, the path under which we scrape ourselves\n\t\t\t\t// should already contain the prefix.\n\t\t\t\tu.Scheme = opts.Scheme\n\t\t\t\tu.Host = opts.Host\n\t\t\t} else {\n\t\t\t\t// Otherwise, we only know that localhost is not reachable\n\t\t\t\t// externally, so we replace only the hostname by the one in the\n\t\t\t\t// external URL. It could be the wrong hostname for the service on\n\t\t\t\t// this port, but it's still the best possible guess.\n\t\t\t\thost, _, err := sanitizeSplitHostPort(opts.Host)\n\t\t\t\tif err != nil {\n\t\t\t\t\treturn u, err\n\t\t\t\t}\n\t\t\t\tu.Host = host\n\t\t\t\tif port != \"\" {\n\t\t\t\t\tu.Host = net.JoinHostPort(u.Host, port)\n\t\t\t\t}\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t\tbreak\n\t\t}\n\t}\n\n\treturn u, nil\n}\n\nfunc (api *API) scrapePools(r *http.Request) apiFuncResult {\n\tnames := api.scrapePoolsRetriever(r.Context()).ScrapePools()\n\tsort.Strings(names)\n\tres := &ScrapePoolsDiscovery{ScrapePools: names}\n\treturn apiFuncResult{data: res, err: nil, warnings: nil, finalizer: nil}\n}\n\nfunc (api *API) targets(r *http.Request) apiFuncResult {\n\tgetSortedPools := func(targets map[string][]*scrape.Target) ([]string, int) {\n\t\tvar n int\n\t\tpools := make([]string, 0, len(targets))\n\t\tfor p, t := range targets {\n\t\t\tpools = append(pools, p)\n\t\t\tn += len(t)\n\t\t}\n\t\tslices.Sort(pools)\n\t\treturn pools, n\n\t}\n\n\tscrapePool := r.URL.Query().Get(\"scrapePool\")\n\tstate := strings.ToLower(r.URL.Query().Get(\"state\"))\n\tshowActive := state == \"\" || state == \"any\" || state == \"active\"\n\tshowDropped := state == \"\" || state == \"any\" || state == \"dropped\"\n\tres := &TargetDiscovery{}\n\tbuilder := labels.NewBuilder(labels.EmptyLabels())\n\n\tif showActive {\n\t\ttargetsActive := api.targetRetriever(r.Context()).TargetsActive()\n\t\tactivePools, numTargets := getSortedPools(targetsActive)\n\t\tres.ActiveTargets = make([]*Target, 0, numTargets)\n\n\t\tfor _, pool := range activePools {\n\t\t\tif scrapePool != \"\" && pool != scrapePool {\n\t\t\t\tcontinue\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t\tfor _, target := range targetsActive[pool] {\n\t\t\t\tlastErrStr := \"\"\n\t\t\t\tlastErr := target.LastError()\n\t\t\t\tif lastErr != nil {\n\t\t\t\t\tlastErrStr = lastErr.Error()\n\t\t\t\t}\n\n\t\t\t\tglobalURL, err := getGlobalURL(target.URL(), api.globalURLOptions)\n\n\t\t\t\tres.ActiveTargets = append(res.ActiveTargets, &Target{\n\t\t\t\t\tDiscoveredLabels: target.DiscoveredLabels(builder),\n\t\t\t\t\tLabels:           target.Labels(builder),\n\t\t\t\t\tScrapePool:       pool,\n\t\t\t\t\tScrapeURL:        target.URL().String(),\n\t\t\t\t\tGlobalURL:        globalURL.String(),\n\t\t\t\t\tLastError: func() string {\n\t\t\t\t\t\tswitch {\n\t\t\t\t\t\tcase err == nil && lastErrStr == \"\":\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\treturn \"\"\n\t\t\t\t\t\tcase err != nil:\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\treturn fmt.Errorf(\"%s: %w\", lastErrStr, err).Error()\n\t\t\t\t\t\tdefault:\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\treturn lastErrStr\n\t\t\t\t\t\t}\n\t\t\t\t\t}(),\n\t\t\t\t\tLastScrape:         target.LastScrape(),\n\t\t\t\t\tLastScrapeDuration: target.LastScrapeDuration().Seconds(),\n\t\t\t\t\tHealth:             target.Health(),\n\t\t\t\t\tScrapeInterval:     target.GetValue(model.ScrapeIntervalLabel),\n\t\t\t\t\tScrapeTimeout:      target.GetValue(model.ScrapeTimeoutLabel),\n\t\t\t\t})\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t}\n\t} else {\n\t\tres.ActiveTargets = []*Target{}\n\t}\n\tif showDropped {\n\t\tres.DroppedTargetCounts = api.targetRetriever(r.Context()).TargetsDroppedCounts()\n\n\t\ttargetsDropped := api.targetRetriever(r.Context()).TargetsDropped()\n\t\tdroppedPools, numTargets := getSortedPools(targetsDropped)\n\t\tres.DroppedTargets = make([]*DroppedTarget, 0, numTargets)\n\t\tfor _, pool := range droppedPools {\n\t\t\tif scrapePool != \"\" && pool != scrapePool {\n\t\t\t\tcontinue\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t\tfor _, target := range targetsDropped[pool] {\n\t\t\t\tres.DroppedTargets = append(res.DroppedTargets, &DroppedTarget{\n\t\t\t\t\tDiscoveredLabels: target.DiscoveredLabels(builder),\n\t\t\t\t\tScrapePool:       pool,\n\t\t\t\t})\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t}\n\t} else {\n\t\tres.DroppedTargets = []*DroppedTarget{}\n\t}\n\treturn apiFuncResult{res, nil, nil, nil}\n}\n\nfunc matchLabels(lset labels.Labels, matchers []*labels.Matcher) bool {\n\tfor _, m := range matchers {\n\t\tif !m.Matches(lset.Get(m.Name)) {\n\t\t\treturn false\n\t\t}\n\t}\n\treturn true\n}\n\nfunc (api *API) targetMetadata(r *http.Request) apiFuncResult {\n\tlimit := -1\n\tif s := r.FormValue(\"limit\"); s != \"\" {\n\t\tvar err error\n\t\tif limit, err = strconv.Atoi(s); err != nil {\n\t\t\treturn apiFuncResult{nil, &apiError{errorBadData, errors.New(\"limit must be a md.Unit,\n\t\t\t\t})\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t}\n\t}\n\n\treturn apiFuncResult{res, nil, nil, nil}\n}\n\ntype metricMetadata struct {\n\tTarget       labels.Labels    `json:\"target\"`\n\tMetricFamily string           `json:\"metric,omitempty\"`\n\tType         model.MetricType `json:\"type\"`\n\tHelp         string           `json:\"help\"`\n\tUnit         string           `json:\"unit\"`\n}\n\n// rules(r *http.Request) apiFuncResult {\n\tif err := r.ParseForm(); err != nil {\n\t\treturn apiFuncResult{nil, &apiError{errorBadData, fmt.Errorf(\"error parsing form values: %w\", err)}, nil,     \"alerting\",\n\t\t\t\t}\n\n\t\t\tcase *rules.RecordingRule:\n\t\t\t\tif !returnRecording {\n\t\t\t\t\tbreak\n\t\t\t\t}\n\t\t\t\tenrichedRule = RecordingRule{\n\t\t\t\t\tName: lastError,\n\t\t\t\t\tEvaluationTime: rule.GetEvaluationDuration().Seconds(),\n\t\t\t\t\tLastEvaluation: rule.GetEvaluationTimestamp(),\n\t\t\t\t\tType: nil {\n\t\treturn apiFuncResult{nil, returnAPIError(set.Err()), warnings, closer}\n\t}\n\n\treturn apiFuncResult{metrics, nil, warnings, closer}\n}\n\nfunc (*API) dropSeries(*http.Request) apiFuncResult {\n\treturn apiFuncResult{nil, &apiError{errorInternal, errors.New(\"not implemented\")}, nil, nil}\n}\n\n// Target has the information for one target.\ntype Target struct {\n\t// Labels before any processing.\n\tDiscoveredLabels labels.Labels `json:\"discoveredLabels\"`\n\t// Any labels that are added to this target and its metrics.\n\tLabels labels.Labels `json:\"labels\"`\n\n\tScrapePool string `json:\"scrapePool\"`\n\tScrapeURL  string `json:\"scrapeUrl\"`\n\tGlobalURL  string `json:\"globalUrl\"`\n\n\tLastError          string              `json:\"lastError\"`\n\tLastScrape         time.Time           `json:\"lastScrape\"`\n\tLastScrapeDuration float64             `json:\"lastScrapeDuration\"`\n\tHealth             scrape.TargetHealth `json:\"health\"`\n\n\tScrapeInterval string `json:\"scrapeInterval\"`\n\tScrapeTimeout  string `json:\"scrapeTimeout\"`\n}\n\ntype ScrapePoolsDiscovery struct {\n\tScrapePools []string `json:\"scrapePools\"`\n}\n\n// DroppedTarget has the information for one target that was dropped during relabelling.\ntype DroppedTarget struct {\n\t// Labels before any processing.\n\tDiscoveredLabels labels.Labels `json:\"discoveredLabels\"`\n\tScrapePool       string        `json:\"scrapePool\"`\n}\n\n// TargetDiscovery has all the active targets.\ntype TargetDiscovery struct {\n\tActiveTargets       []*Target        `json:\"activeTargets\"`\n\tDroppedTargets      []*DroppedTarget `json:\"droppedTargets\"`\n\tDroppedTargetCounts map[string]int   `json:\"droppedTargetCounts\"`\n}\n\n// GlobalURLOptions contains fields used for deriving the global URL for local targets.\ntype GlobalURLOptions struct {\n\tListenAddress string\n\tHost          string\n\tScheme        string\n}\n\n// sanitizeSplitHostPort acts like net.SplitHostPort.\n// Additionally, if there is no port in the host passed as input, we return the\n// original host, making sure that IPv6 addresses are not surrounded by square\n// brackets.\nfunc sanitizeSplitHostPort(input string) (string, string, error) {\n\thost, port, err := net.SplitHostPort(input)\n\tif err != nil && strings.HasSuffix(err.Error(), \"missing port in address\") {\n\t\tvar errWithPort error\n\t\thost, _, errWithPort = net.SplitHostPort(input + \":80\")\n\t\tif errWithPort == nil {\n\t\t\terr = nil\n\t\t}\n\t}\n\treturn host, port, err\n}\n\nfunc getGlobalURL(u *url.URL, opts GlobalURLOptions) (*url.URL, error) {\n\thost, port, err := sanitizeSplitHostPort(u.Host)\n\tif err != nil {\n\t\treturn u, err\n\t}\n\n\tfor _, lhr := range LocalhostRepresentations {\n\t\tif host == lhr {\n\t\t\t_, ownPort, err := net.SplitHostPort(opts.ListenAddress)\n\t\t\tif err != nil {\n\t\t\t\treturn u, err\n\t\t\t}\n\n\t\t\tif port == ownPort {\n\t\t\t\t// Only in the case where the target is on localhost and its port is\n\t\t\t\t// the same as the one we're listening on, we know for sure that\n\t\t\t\t// we're monitoring our own process and that we need to change the\n\t\t\t\t// scheme, hostname, and port to the externally reachable ones as\n\t\t\t\t// well. We shouldn't need to touch the path at all, since if a\n\t\t\t\t// path prefix is defined, the path under which we scrape ourselves\n\t\t\t\t// should already contain the prefix.\n\t\t\t\tu.Scheme = opts.Scheme\n\t\t\t\tu.Host = opts.Host\n\t\t\t} else {\n\t\t\t\t// Otherwise, we only know that localhost is not reachable\n\t\t\t\t// externally, so we replace only the hostname by the one in the\n\t\t\t\t// external URL. It could be the wrong hostname for the service on\n\t\t\t\t// this port, but it's still the best possible guess.\n\t\t\t\thost, _, err := sanitizeSplitHostPort(opts.Host)\n\t\t\t\tif err != nil {\n\t\t\t\t\treturn u, err\n\t\t\t\t}\n\t\t\t\tu.Host = host\n\t\t\t\tif port != \"\" {\n\t\t\t\t\tu.Host = net.JoinHostPort(u.Host, port)\n\t\t\t\t}\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t\tbreak\n\t\t}\n\t}\n\n\treturn u, nil\n}\n\nfunc (api *API) scrapePools(r *http.Request) apiFuncResult {\n\tnames := api.scrapePoolsRetriever(r.Context()).ScrapePools()\n\tsort.Strings(names)\n\tres := `json:\"droppedTargetCounts\"`\n}\n\n// GlobalURLOptions contains fields used for deriving the global URL for local targets.\ntype GlobalURLOptions struct {\n\tListenAddress string\n\tHost          string\n\tScheme        string\n}\n\n// sanitizeSplitHostPort acts like net.SplitHostPort.\n// Additionally, if there is no port in the host passed as input, we return the\n// original host, making sure that IPv6 addresses are not surrounded by square\n// brackets.\nfunc sanitizeSplitHostPort(input string) (string, string, error) {\n\thost, port, err := net.SplitHostPort(input)\n\tif err != nil && strings.HasSuffix(err.Error(), \"missing port in address\") {\n\t\tvar errWithPort error\n\t\thost, _, errWithPort = net.SplitHostPort(input + \":80\")\n\t\tif errWithPort == nil {\n\t\t\terr = nil\n\t\t}\n\t}\n\treturn host, port, err\n}\n\nfunc getGlobalURL(u *url.URL, opts GlobalURLOptions) (*url.URL, error) {\n\thost, port, err := sanitizeSplitHostPort(u.Host)\n\tif err != nil {\n\t\treturn u, err\n\t}\n\n\tfor _, lhr := range LocalhostRepresentations {\n\t\tif host == lhr {\n\t\t\t_, ownPort, err := net.SplitHostPort(opts.ListenAddress)\n\t\t\tif err != nil {\n\t\t\t\treturn u, err\n\t\t\t}\n\n\t\t\tif port == ownPort {\n\t\t\t\t// Only in the case where the target is on localhost and its port is\n\t\t\t\t// the same as the one we're listening on, we know for sure that\n\t\t\t\t// we're monitoring our own process and that we need to change the\n\t\t\t\t// scheme, hostname, and port to the externally reachable ones as\n\t\t\t\t// well. We shouldn't need to touch the path at all, since if a\n\t\t\t\t// path prefix is defined, the path under which we scrape ourselves\n\t\t\t\t// should already contain the prefix.\n\t\t\t\tu.Scheme = opts.Scheme\n\t\t\t\tu.Host = opts.Host\n\t\t\t} else {\n\t\t\t\t// Otherwise, we only know that localhost is not reachable\n\t\t\t\t// externally, so we replace only the hostname by the one in the\n\t\t\t\t// external URL. It could be the wrong hostname for the service on\n\t\t\t\t// this port, but it's still the best possible guess.\n\t\t\t\thost, _, err := sanitizeSplitHostPort(opts.Host)\n\t\t\t\tif err != nil {\n\t\t\t\t\treturn u, err\n\t\t\t\t}\n\t\t\t\tu.Host = host\n\t\t\t\tif port != \"\" {\n\t\t\t\t\tu.Host = net.JoinHostPort(u.Host, port)\n\t\t\t\t}\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t\tbreak\n\t\t}\n\t}\n\n\treturn u, nil\n}\n\nfunc (api *API) scrapePools(r *http.Request) apiFuncResult {\n\tnames := api.scrapePoolsRetriever(r.Context()).ScrapePools()\n\tsort.Strings(names)\n\tres := {\n\t\tres.DroppedTargets = []*DroppedTarget{}\n\t}\n\treturn apiFuncResult{res, nil, nil, nil}\n}\n\nfunc matchLabels(lset labels.Labels, matchers []*labels.Matcher) bool {\n\tfor _, m := range matchers {\n\t\tif !m.Matches(lset.Get(m.Name)) {\n\t\t\treturn false\n\t\t}\n\t}\n\treturn true\n}\n\nfunc (api *API) targetMetadata(r *http.Request) apiFuncResult {\n\tlimit := -1\n\tif s := `json:\"evaluationTime\"`\n\tLastEvaluation time.Time        `json:\"lastEvaluation\"`\n\t// Type of a recordingRule is always \"recording\".\n\tType string `json:\"type\"`\n}\n\nfunc (api *API) rules(r *http.Request) apiFuncResult {\n\tif err := r.ParseForm(); err != nil {\n\t\treturn apiFuncResult{nil, &apiError{errorBadData, fmt.Errorf(\"error parsing form values: %w\", err)}, nil, nil}\n\t}\n\n\tqueryFormToSet := func(values []string) map[string]struct{} {\n\t\tset := make(map[string]struct{}, len(values))\n\t\tfor _, v := range values {\n\t\t\tset[v] = struct{}{}\n\t\t}\n\t\treturn set\n\t}\n\n\trnSet := queryFormToSet(r.Form[\"rule_name[]\"])\n\trgSet := queryFormToSet(r.Form[\"rule_group[]\"])\n\tfSet := queryFormToSet(r.Form[\"file[]\"])\n\n\tmatcherSets, err := parseMatchersParam(r.Form[\"match[]\"])\n\tif err != nil {\n\t\treturn apiFuncResult{nil, &apiError{errorBadData, err}, nil, nil}\n\t}\n\n\truleGroups := api.rulesRetriever(r.Context()).RuleGroups()\n\tres := &RuleDiscovery{RuleGroups: make([]*RuleGroup, 0, len(ruleGroups))}\n\ttyp := strings.ToLower(r.URL.Query().Get(\"type\"))\n\n\tif typ != \"\" && typ != \"alert\" && typ != \"record\" {\n\t\treturn invalidParamError(fmt.Errorf(\"not supported value %q\", typ), \"type\")\n\t}\n\n\treturnAlerts := typ == \"\" || typ == \"alert\"\n\treturnRecording := typ == \"\" || typ == \"record\"\n\n\texcludeAlerts, err := parseExcludeAlerts(r)\n\tif err != nil {\n\t\treturn invalidParamError(err, \"exclude_alerts\")\n\t}\n\n\tmaxGroups, nextToken, parseErr := parseListRulesPaginationRequest(r)\n\tif parseErr != nil {\n\t\treturn *parseErr\n\t}\n\n\trgs := make([]*RuleGroup, 0, len(ruleGroups))\n\n\tfoundToken := false\n\n\tfor _, grp := range ruleGroups {\n\t\tif maxGroups > 0 && nextToken != \"\" && !foundToken {\n\t\t\tif nextToken != getRuleGroupNextToken(grp.File(), grp.Name()) {\n\t\t\t\tcontinue\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t\tfoundToken = true\n\t\t}\n\n\t\tif len(rgSet) > 0 {\n\t\t\tif _, ok := rgSet[grp.Name()]; !ok {\n\t\t\t\tcontinue\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t}\n\n\t\tif len(fSet) > 0 {\n\t\t\tif _, ok := fSet[grp.File()]; !ok {\n\t\t\t\tcontinue\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t}\n\n\t\tapiRuleGroup := &RuleGroup{\n\t\t\tName:           grp.Name(),\n\t\t\tFile:           grp.File(),\n\t\t\tInterval:       grp.Interval().Seconds(),\n\t\t\tLimit:          grp.Limit(),\n\t\t\tRules:          []Rule{},\n\t\t\tEvaluationTime: grp.GetEvaluationTime().Seconds(),\n\t\t\tLastEvaluation: grp.GetLastEvaluation(),\n\t\t}\n\n\t\tfor _, rr := range grp.Rules(matcherSets...) {\n\t\t\tvar enrichedRule Rule\n\n\t\t\tif len(rnSet) > 0 {\n\t\t\t\tif _, ok := rnSet[rr.Name()]; !ok {\n\t\t\t\t\tcontinue\n\t\t\t\t}\n\t\t\t}\n\n\t\t\tlastError := \"\"\n\t\t\tif rr.LastError() != nil {\n\t\t\t\tlastError = rr.LastError().Error()\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t\tswitch rule := rr.(type) {\n\t\t\tcase *rules.AlertingRule:\n\t\t\t\tif !returnAlerts {\n\t\t\t\t\tbreak\n\t\t\t\t}\n\t\t\t\tvar activeAlerts []*Alert\n\t\t\t\tif !excludeAlerts {\n\t\t\t\t\tactiveAlerts = rulesAlertsToAPIAlerts(rule.ActiveAlerts())\n\t\t\t\t}\n\n\t\t\t\tenrichedRule = AlertingRule{\n\t\t\t\t\tState:          rule.State().String(),\n\t\t\t\t\tName:           rule.Name(),\n\t\t\t\t\tQuery:          rule.Query().String(),\n\t\t\t\t\tDuration:       rule.HoldDuration().Seconds(),\n\t\t\t\t\tKeepFiringFor:  rule.KeepFiringFor().Seconds(),\n\t\t\t\t\tLabels:         rule.Labels(),\n\t\t\t\t\tAnnotations:    rule.Annotations(),\n\t\t\t\t\tAlerts:         activeAlerts,\n\t\t\t\t\tHealth:         rule.Health(),\n\t\t\t\t\tLastError:      lastError,\n\t\t\t\t\tEvaluationTime: rule.GetEvaluationDuration().Seconds(),\n\t\t\t\t\tLastEvaluation: rule.GetEvaluationTimestamp(),\n\t\t\t\t\tType:           \"alerting\",\n\t\t\t\t}\n\n\t\t\tcase *rules.RecordingRule:\n\t\t\t\tif !returnRecording {\n\t\t\t\t\tbreak\n\t\t\t\t}\n\t\t\t\tenrichedRule = RecordingRule{\n\t\t\t\t\tName:           rule.Name(),\n\t\t\t\t\tQuery:          rule.Query().String(),\n\t\t\t\t\tLabels:         rule.Labels(),\n\t\t\t\t\tHealth:         rule.Health(),\n\t\t\t\t\tLastError:      lastError,\n\t\t\t\t\tEvaluationTime: rule.GetEvaluationDuration().Seconds(),\n\t\t\t\t\tLastEvaluation: rule.GetEvaluationTimestamp(),\n\t\t\t\t\tType:           \"recording\",\n\t\t\t\t}\n\t\t\tdefault:\n\t\t\t\terr := fmt.Errorf(\"failed to assert type of rule '%v'\", rule.Name())\n\t\t\t\treturn apiFuncResult{nil, &apiError{errorInternal, err}, nil, nil}\n\t\t\t}\n\n\t\t\tif enrichedRule != nil {\n\t\t\t\tapiRuleGroup.Rules = append(apiRuleGroup.Rules, enrichedRule)\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t}\n\n\t\t// If the rule group response has no rules, skip it - this means we filtered all the rules of this group.\n\t\tif len(apiRuleGroup.Rules) > 0 {\n\t\t\tif maxGroups > 0 && len(rgs) == int(maxGroups) {\n\t\t\t\t// We've reached the capacity of our page plus one. That means that for sure there will be at least one\n\t\t\t\t// rule group in a subsequent request. Therefore a next token is required.\n\t\t\t\tres.GroupNextToken = getRuleGroupNextToken(grp.File(), grp.Name())\n\t\t\t\tbreak\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t\trgs = append(rgs, apiRuleGroup)\n\t\t}\n\t}\n\n\tif maxGroups > 0 && nextToken != \"\" && !foundToken {\n\t\treturn invalidParamError(fmt.Errorf(\"invalid group_next_token '%v'. were rule groups changed?\", nextToken), \"group_next_token\")\n\t}\n\n\tres.RuleGroups = rgs\n\treturn apiFuncResult{res, nil, nil, nil}\n}\n\nfunc parseExcludeAlerts(r *http.Request) (bool, error) {\n\texcludeAlertsParam := strings.ToLower(r.URL.Query().Get(\"exclude_alerts\"))\n\n\tif excludeAlertsParam == \"\" {\n\t\treturn false, nil\n\t}\n\n\texcludeAlerts, err := strconv.ParseBool(excludeAlertsParam)\n\tif err != nil {\n\t\treturn false, fmt.Errorf(\"error converting exclude_alerts: %w\", err)\n\t}\n\treturn excludeAlerts, nil\n}\n\nfunc parseListRulesPaginationRequest(r *http.Request) (int64, string, *apiFuncResult) {\n\tvar (\n\t\tparsedMaxGroups int64 = -1\n\t\terr             error\n\t)\n\tmaxGroups := r.URL.Query().Get(\"group_limit\")\n\tnextToken := r.URL.Query().Get(\"group_next_token\")\n\n\tif nextToken != \"\" && maxGroups == \"\" {\n\t\terrResult := invalidParamError(errors.New(\"group_limit needs to be present in order to paginate over the groups\"), \"group_next_token\")\n\t\treturn -1, \"\", &errResult\n\t}\n\n\tif maxGroups != \"\" {\n\t\tparsedMaxGroups, err = strconv.ParseInt(maxGroups, 10, 32)\n\t\tif err != nil {\n\t\t\terrResult := invalidParamError(fmt.Errorf(\"group_limit needs to be a valid number: %w\", err), \"group_limit\")\n\t\t\treturn -1, \"\", &errResult\n\t\t}\n\t\tif parsedMaxGroups <= 0 {\n\t\t\terrResult := invalidParamError(errors.New(\"group_limit needs to be greater than 0\"), \"group_limit\")\n\t\t\treturn -1, \"\", &errResult\n\t\t}\n\t}\n\n\tif parsedMaxGroups > 0 {\n\t\treturn parsedMaxGroups, nextToken, nil\n\t}\n\n\treturn -1, \"\", nil\n}\n\nfunc getRuleGroupNextToken(file, group string) string {\n\th := sha1.New()\n\th.Write([]byte(file + \";\" + group))\n\treturn hex.EncodeToString(h.Sum(nil))\n}\n\ntype prometheusConfig struct {\n\tYAML string `json:\"yaml\"`\n}\n\nfunc (api *API) serveRuntimeInfo(*http.Request) apiFuncResult {\n\tstatus, err := \"limit\")\n\t}\n\tts, err := parseTimeParam(r, \"time\", api.now())\n\tif err != nil {\n\t\treturn invalidParamError(err, \"time\")\n\t}\n\tctx := r.Context()\n\tif to := r.FormValue(\"timeout\"); to != \"\" {\n\t\tvar cancel context.CancelFunc\n\t\ttimeout, err := parseDuration(to)\n\t\tif err != nil {\n\t\t\treturn invalidParamError(err, \"timeout\")\n\t\t}\n\n\t\tctx, cancel = *http.Request) (result apiFuncResult) {\n\tlimit, err := parseLimitParam(r.FormValue(\"limit\"))\n\tif err != nil {\n\t\treturn invalidParamError(err, \"limit\")\n\t}\n\tstart, err := parseTime(r.FormValue(\"start\"))\n\tif err != nil {\n\t\treturn invalidParamError(err, \"start\")\n\t}\n\tend, err := parseTime(r.FormValue(\"end\"))\n\tif err != nil {\n\t\treturn invalidParamError(err, \"end\")\n\t}\n\tif end.Before(start) {\n\t\treturn invalidParamError(errors.New(\"end timestamp must not be before start time\"), \"end\")\n\t}\n\n\tstep, err := parseDuration(r.FormValue(\"step\"))\n\tif err != nil {\n\t\treturn invalidParamError(err, \"step\")\n\t}\n\n\tif step <= 0 {\n\t\treturn invalidParamError(errors.New(\"zero or negative query resolution step widths are not accepted. Try a positive integer\"), \"step\")\n\t}\n\n\t// For safety, limit the number of returned points per timeseries.\n\t// This is sufficient for 60s resolution for a week or 1h resolution for a year.\n\tif end.Sub(start)/step > 11000 {\n\t\terr := errors.New(\"exceeded maximum resolution of 11,000 points per timeseries. Try decreasing the query resolution (?step=XX)\")\n\t\treturn apiFuncResult{nil, &apiError{errorBadData, err}, nil, nil}\n\t}\n\n\tctx := r.Context()\n\tif to := r.FormValue(\"timeout\"); to != \"\" {\n\t\tvar cancel context.CancelFunc\n\t\ttimeout, err := parseDuration(to)\n\t\tif err != nil {\n\t\t\treturn invalidParamError(err, \"timeout\")\n\t\t}\n\n\t\tctx, cancel = context.WithTimeout(ctx, timeout)\n\t\tdefer cancel()\n\t}\n\n\topts, err := extractQueryOpts(r)\n\tif err != nil {\n\t\treturn apiFuncResult{nil, &apiError{errorBadData, err}, nil, nil}\n\t}\n\tqry, err := api.QueryEngine.NewRangeQuery(ctx, api.Queryable, opts, r.FormValue(\"query\"), start, end, step)\n\tif err != nil {\n\t\treturn invalidParamError(err, \"query\")\n\t}\n\t// From now on, we must only return with a finalizer in the result (to\n\t// be called by the caller) or call qry.Close ourselves (which is\n\t// required in the case of a panic).\n\tdefer func() {\n\t\tif result.finalizer == nil {\n\t\t\tqry.Close()\n\t\t}\n\t}()\n\n\tctx = httputil.ContextFromRequest(ctx, r)\n\n\tres := qry.Exec(ctx)\n\tif res.Err != nil {\n\t\treturn apiFuncResult{nil, returnAPIError(res.Err), res.Warnings, qry.Close}\n\t}\n\n\twarnings := res.Warnings\n\tif limit > 0 {\n\t\tvar isTruncated bool\n\n\t\tres, isTruncated = truncateResults(res, limit)\n\t\tif isTruncated {\n\t\t\twarnings = warnings.Add(errors.New(\"results truncated due to limit\"))\n\t\t}\n\t}\n\n\t// Optional stats field in response if parameter \"stats\" is not empty.\n\tsr := api.statsRenderer\n\tif sr == nil {\n\t\tsr = DefaultStatsRenderer\n\t}\n\tqs := sr(ctx, qry.Stats(), r.FormValue(\"stats\"))\n\n\treturn apiFuncResult{&QueryData{\n\t\tResultType: res.Value.Type(),\n\t\tResult:     res.Value,\n\t\tStats:      qs,\n\t}, nil, warnings, qry.Close}\n}\n\nfunc (api *API) queryExemplars(r *http.Request) apiFuncResult {\n\tstart, err := parseTimeParam(r, \"start\", MinTime)\n\tif err != nil {\n\t\treturn invalidParamError(err, \"start\")\n\t}\n\tend, err := parseTimeParam(r, \"end\", MaxTime)\n\tif err != nil {\n\t\treturn invalidParamError(err, \"end\")\n\t}\n\tif returnAPIError(err), nil, nil}\n\t}\n\n\treturn apiFuncResult{res, nil, nil, nil}\n}\n\nfunc returnAPIError(err error) *apiError {\n\tif err == nil {\n\t\treturn nil\n\t}\n\n\tvar eqc promql.ErrQueryCanceled\n\tvar eqt promql.ErrQueryTimeout\n\tvar es promql.ErrStorage\n\tswitch {\n\tcase errors.As(err, &eqc):\n\t\treturn &apiError{errorCanceled, err}\n\tcase errors.As(err, &eqt):\n\t\treturn &apiError{errorTimeout, err}\n\tcase errors.As(err, &es):\n\t\treturn &apiError{errorInternal, err}\n\t}\n\n\tif errors.Is(err, context.Canceled) {\n\t\treturn &apiError{errorCanceled, err}\n\t}\n\n\treturn &apiError{errorExec, err}\n}\n\nfunc (api *API) labelNames(r *http.Request) apiFuncResult {\n\tlimit, err := string\n\tScheme        string\n}\n\n// sanitizeSplitHostPort acts like net.SplitHostPort.\n// Additionally, if there is no port in the host passed as input, we return the\n// original host, making sure that IPv6 addresses are not surrounded by square\n// brackets.\nfunc sanitizeSplitHostPort(input string) (string, string, error) {\n\thost, port, err := net.SplitHostPort(input)\n\tif err != nil && strings.HasSuffix(err.Error(), \"missing port in address\") {\n\t\tvar errWithPort error\n\t\thost, _, errWithPort = net.SplitHostPort(input + \":80\")\n\t\tif errWithPort == nil {\n\t\t\terr = nil\n\t\t}\n\t}\n\treturn host, port, err\n}\n\nfunc getGlobalURL(u *url.URL, opts GlobalURLOptions) (*url.URL, error) {\n\thost, port, err := sanitizeSplitHostPort(u.Host)\n\tif err != nil {\n\t\treturn u, err\n\t}\n\n\tfor _, lhr := range LocalhostRepresentations {\n\t\tif host == lhr {\n\t\t\t_, ownPort, err := net.SplitHostPort(opts.ListenAddress)\n\t\t\tif err != nil {\n\t\t\t\treturn u, err\n\t\t\t}\n\n\t\t\tif port == ownPort {\n\t\t\t\t// Only in the case where the target is on localhost and its port is\n\t\t\t\t// the same as the one we're listening on, we know for sure that\n\t\t\t\t// we're monitoring our own process and that we need to change the\n\t\t\t\t// scheme, hostname, and port to the externally reachable ones as\n\t\t\t\t// well. We shouldn't need to touch the path at all, since if a\n\t\t\t\t// path prefix is defined, the path under which we scrape ourselves\n\t\t\t\t// should already contain the prefix.\n\t\t\t\tu.Scheme = opts.Scheme\n\t\t\t\tu.Host = opts.Host\n\t\t\t} else {\n\t\t\t\t// Otherwise, we only know that localhost is not reachable\n\t\t\t\t// externally, so we replace only the hostname by the one in the\n\t\t\t\t// external URL. It could be the wrong hostname for the service on\n\t\t\t\t// this port, but it's still the best possible guess.\n\t\t\t\thost, _, err := sanitizeSplitHostPort(opts.Host)\n\t\t\t\tif err != nil {\n\t\t\t\t\treturn u, err\n\t\t\t\t}\n\t\t\t\tu.Host = host\n\t\t\t\tif port != \"\" {\n\t\t\t\t\tu.Host = net.JoinHostPort(u.Host, port)\n\t\t\t\t}\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t\tbreak\n\t\t}\n\t}\n\n\treturn u, nil\n}\n\nfunc (api *API) scrapePools(r *http.Request) apiFuncResult {\n\tnames := api.scrapePoolsRetriever(r.Context()).ScrapePools()\n\tsort.Strings(names)\n\tres := rules(r *http.Request) apiFuncResult {\n\tif err := r.ParseForm(); err != nil {\n\t\treturn apiFuncResult{nil, &apiError{errorBadData, fmt.Errorf(\"error parsing form values: %w\", err)}, nil, \"group_next_token\")\n\t}\n\n\tres.RuleGroups = rgs\n\treturn apiFuncResult{res, nil, nil, nil}\n}\n\nfunc parseExcludeAlerts(r *http.Request) (bool, error) {\n\texcludeAlertsParam := (api *API) notificationsSSE(w http.ResponseWriter, r *http.Request) {\n\thttputil.SetCORS(w, api.CORSOrigin, r)\n\tw.Header().Set(\"Content-Type\", package v1

import (
	"encoding/json"
	"fmt"
	"io"
	"net/http"
	"sync"
	"time"

	"github.com/oklog/ulid/v2"
)

// Matcher represents a label matcher for silence matching.
type Matcher struct {
	Name    string `json:"name"`
	Value   string `json:"value"`
	IsRegex bool   `json:"isRegex"`
}

// Silence represents a single silence for alerting.
type Silence struct {
	ID        string     `json:"id"`
	Matchers  []Matcher  `json:"matchers"`
	StartsAt  time.Time  `json:"startsAt"`
	EndsAt    time.Time  `json:"endsAt"`
	CreatedBy string     `json:"createdBy"`
	Comment   string     `json:"comment"`
}

// SilenceRequest represents a silence request (without ID).
type SilenceRequest struct {
	Matchers  []Matcher `json:"matchers"`
	StartsAt  time.Time `json:"startsAt"`
	EndsAt    time.Time `json:"endsAt"`
	CreatedBy string    `json:"createdBy"`
	Comment   string    `json:"comment"`
}

// SilenceStore provides in-memory storage for silences.
type SilenceStore struct {
	mu       sync.RWMutex
	silences map[string]*Silence
}

// NewSilenceStore creates a new silence store.
func NewSilenceStore() *SilenceStore {
	return &SilenceStore{
		silences: make(map[string]*Silence),
	}
}

		silenceStore: NewSilenceStore(),

	}

			Comment:   "Test silence 1",
		},
		{
			Matchers: []Matcher{
				{Name: "alertname", Value: "TestAlert2", IsRegex: false},
			},
			StartsAt:  startTime,
			EndsAt:    endTime,
			CreatedBy: "test-user",
			Comment:   "Test silence 2",
		},
	}

	body, err := json.Marshal(requests)
	require.NoError(t, err)

	r := httptest.NewRequest("POST", "/api/v1/silences/bulk", bytes.NewReader(body))
	w := httptest.NewRecorder()

	api.silenceBulk(r)

	resp := w.Header()
	require.NoError(t, err)
	require.Equal(t, "success", resp.Get("X-Mock-Status"))

	// Parse the response
	result := api.silenceBulk(r

6. EDIT /workspace/web/api/v1/silences_bulk_test.go
Before
func TestSilenceBulkSuccess(t *testing.T) {
	api := &API{
		silenceStore: NewSilenceStore(),
		ready:        func(f http.HandlerFunc) http.HandlerFunc { return f },
	}

	now := time.Now()
	startTime := now.Add(1 * time.Hour)
	endTime := now.Add(2 * time.Hour)

	requests := []SilenceRequest{
		{
			Matchers: []Matcher{
				{Name: "alertname", Value: "TestAlert1", IsRegex: false},
			},
			StartsAt:  startTime,
			EndsAt:    endTime,
			CreatedBy: "test-user",
			Comment:   "Test silence 1",
		},
		{
			Matchers: []Matcher{
				{Name: "alertname", Value: "TestAlert2", IsRegex: false},
			},
			StartsAt:  startTime,
			EndsAt:    endTime,
			CreatedBy: "test-user",
			Comment:   "Test silence 2",
		},
	}

	body, err := json.Marshal(requests)
	require.NoError(t, err)

	r := httptest.NewRequest("POST", "/api/v1/silences/bulk", bytes.NewReader(body))
	w := httptest.NewRecorder()

	api.silenceBulk(r)

	resp := w.Header()
	require.NoError(t, err)
	require.Equal(t, "success", resp.Get("X-Mock-Status"))

	// Parse the response
	result := api.silenceBulk(r)
	require.NoError(t, result.err)

	response := result.data.(*BulkSilenceResponse)
	require.Len(t, response.IDs, 2)

	// Verify that silences were actually created
	for _, id := range response.IDs {
		require.NotEmpty(t, id)
	}
}
After
func TestSilenceBulkSuccess(t *testing.T) {
	api := &API{
		silenceStore: NewSilenceStore(),
		ready:        func(f http.HandlerFunc) http.HandlerFunc { return f },
	}

	now := time.Now()
	startTime := now.Add(1 * time.Hour)
	endTime := now.Add(2 * time.Hour)

	requests := []SilenceRequest{
		{
			Matchers: []Matcher{
				{Name: "alertname", Value: "TestAlert1", IsRegex: false},
			},
			StartsAt:  startTime,
			EndsAt:    endTime,
			CreatedBy: "test-user",
			Comment:   "Test silence 1",
		},
		{
			Matchers: []Matcher{
				{Name: "alertname", Value: "TestAlert2", IsRegex: false},
			},
			StartsAt:  startTime,
			EndsAt:    endTime,
			CreatedBy: "test-user",
			Comment:   "Test silence 2",
		},
	}

	body, err := json.Marshal(requests)
	require.NoError(t, err)

	r := httptest.NewRequest("POST", "/api/v1/silences/bulk", bytes.NewReader(body))
	result := api.silenceBulk(r)

	require.NoError(t, result.err)

	response := result.data.(*BulkSilenceResponse)
	require.Len(t, response.IDs, 2)

	// Verify that silences were actually created
	for _, id := range response.IDs {
		require.NotEmpty(t, id)
	}
}
